/bin/mkdir -p /usr/share/info
f=nettle.info ; \
[ -f $f ] || f="./$f" ; \
/usr/bin/install -c -m 644 "$f" /usr/share/info ; \
if (install-info --version && \
    install-info --version 2>&1 | sed 1q | grep -i -v debian) >/dev/null 2>&1; then \
  install-info --info-dir="/usr/share/info" "$f" ; \
else : ; fi
